Gauss Agent - Development Guide","","Instructions for AI coding assistants and developers working on the gauss-agent codebase.","","## Development Environment","","```bash","source .venv/bin/activate  # ALWAYS activate before running Python","```","","## Project Structure","","```","gauss-agent/","├── run_agent.py          # AIAgent class — core conversation loop","├── model_tools.py        # Tool orchestration, _discover_tools(), handle_function_call()","├── toolsets.py           # Toolset definitions, _GAUSS_CORE_TOOLS list","├── cli.py                # GaussCLI class — interactive CLI orchestrator","├── gauss_state.py       # SessionDB — SQLite session store (FTS5 search)","├── agent/                # Agent internals","│   ├── prompt_builder.py     # System prompt assembly","│   ├── context_compressor.py # Auto context compression","│   ├── prompt_caching.py     # Anthropic prompt caching","│   ├── auxiliary_client.py   # Auxiliary LLM client (vision, summarization)","│   ├── model_metadata.py     # Model context lengths, token estimation","│   ├── display.py            # KawaiiSpinner, tool preview formatting","│   ├── skill_commands.py     # Skill slash commands (shared CLI/gateway)","│   └── trajectory.py         # Trajectory saving helpers","├── gauss_cli/           # CLI subcommands and setup","│   ├── main.py           # Entry point — all `gauss` subcommands","│   ├── config.py         # DEFAULT_CONFIG, OPTIONAL_ENV_VARS, migration","│   ├── commands.py       # Slash command definitions + SlashCommandCompleter","│   ├── callbacks.py      # Terminal callbacks (clarify, sudo, approval)","│   ├── setup.py          # Interactive setup wizard","│   ├── skin_engine.py    # Skin/theme engine — CLI visual customization","│   ├── skills_config.py  # `gauss skills` — enable/disable skills per platform","│   ├── tools_config.py   # `gauss tools` — enable/disable tools per platform","│   ├── skills_hub.py     # `/skills` slash command (search, browse, install)","│   ├── models.py         # Model catalog, provider model lists","│   └── auth.py           # Provider credential resolution","├── tools/                # Tool implementations (one file per tool)","│   ├── registry.py       # Central tool registry (schemas, handlers, dispatch)","│   ├── approval.py       # Dangerous command detection","│   ├── terminal_tool.py  # Terminal orchestration","│   ├── process_registry.py # Background process management","│   ├── file_tools.py     # File read/write/search/patch","│   ├── web_tools.py      # Firecrawl search/extract","│   ├── browser_tool.py   # Browserbase browser automation","│   ├── code_execution_tool.py # execute_code sandbox","│   ├── delegate_tool.py  # Subagent delegation","│   ├── mcp_tool.py       # MCP client (~1050 lines)","│   └── environments/     # Terminal backends (local, docker, ssh, modal, daytona, singularity)","├── gateway/              # Messaging platform gateway","│   ├── run.py            # Main loop, slash commands, message dispatch","│   ├── session.py        # SessionStore — conversation persistence","│   └── platforms/        # Adapters: telegram, discord, slack, whatsapp, homeassistant, signal","├── acp_adapter/          # ACP server (VS Code / Zed / JetBrains integration)","├── cron/                 # Scheduler (jobs.py, scheduler.py)","├── environments/         # RL training environments (Atropos)","├── tests/                # Pytest suite (~3000 tests)","└── batch_runner.py       # Parallel batch processing","```","","**User config:** `~/.gauss/config.yaml` (settings), `~/.gauss/.env` (API keys)","","## File Dependency Chain","","```","tools/registry.py  (no deps — imported by all tool files)","       ↑","tools/*.py  (each calls registry.register() at import time)","       ↑","model_tools.py  (imports tools/registry + triggers tool discovery)","       ↑","run_agent.py, cli.py, batch_runner.py, environments/","```","","---","","## AIAgent Class (run_agent.py)","","```python","class AIAgent:","    def __init__(self,","        model: str = \"anthropic/claude-opus-4.6\",","        max_iterations: int = 90,","        enabled_toolsets: list = None,","        disabled_toolsets: list = None,","        quiet_mode: bool = False,","        save_trajectories: bool = False,","        platform: str = None,           # \"cli\", \"telegram\", etc.","        session_id: str = None,","        skip_context_files: bool = False,","        skip_memory: bool = False,","        # ... plus provider, api_mode, callbacks, routing params","    ): ...","","    def chat(self, message: str) -\u003e str:","        \"\"\"Simple interface — returns final response string.\"\"\"","","    def run_conversation(self, user_message: str, system_message: str = None,","                         conversation_history: list = None, task_id: str = None) -\u003e dict:","        \"\"\"Full interface — returns dict with final_response + messages.\"\"\"","```","","### Agent Loop","","The core loop is inside `run_conversation()` — entirely synchronous:","","```python","while api_call_count \u003c self.max_iterations and self.iteration_budget.remaining \u003e 0:","    response = client.chat.completions.create(model=model, messages=messages, tools=tool_schemas)","    if response.tool_calls:","        for tool_call in response.tool_calls:","            result = handle_function_call(tool_call.name, tool_call.args, task_id)","            messages.append(tool_result_message(result))","        api_call_count += 1","    else:","        return response.content","```","","Messages follow OpenAI format: `{\"role\": \"system/user/assistant/tool\", ...}`. Reasoning content is stored in `assistant_msg[\"reasoning\"]`.","","---","","## CLI Architecture (cli.py)","","- **Rich** for banner/panels, **prompt_toolkit** for input with autocomplete","- **KawaiiSpinner** (`agent/display.py`) — animated faces during API calls, `┊` activity feed for tool results","- `load_cli_config()` in cli.py merges hardcoded defaults + user config YAML","- **Skin engine** (`gauss_cli/skin_engine.py`) — data-driven CLI theming; initialized from `display.skin` config key at startup; skins customize banner colors, spinner faces/verbs/wings, tool prefix, response box, branding text","- `process_command()` is a method on `GaussCLI` (not in commands.py)","- Skill slash commands: `agent/skill_commands.py` scans `~/.gauss/skills/`, injects as **user message** (not system prompt) to preserve prompt caching","","### Adding CLI Commands","","1. Add to `COMMANDS` dict in `gauss_cli/commands.py`","2. Add handler in `GaussCLI.process_command()` in `cli.py`","3. For persistent settings, use `save_config_value()` in `cli.py`","","---","","## Adding New Tools","","Requires changes in **3 files**:","","**1. Create `tools/your_tool.py`:**","```python","import json, os","from tools.registry import registry","","def check_requirements() -\u003e bool:","    return bool(os.getenv(\"EXAMPLE_API_KEY\"))","","def example_tool(param: str, task_id: str = None) -\u003e str:","    return json.dumps({\"success\": True, \"data\": \"...\"})","","registry.register(","    name=\"example_tool\",","    toolset=\"example\",","    schema={\"name\": \"example_tool\", \"description\": \"...\", \"parameters\": {...}},","    handler=lambda args, **kw: example_tool(param=args.get(\"param\", \"\"), task_id=kw.get(\"task_id\")),","    check_fn=check_requirements,","    requires_env=[\"EXAMPLE_API_KEY\"],",")","```","","**2. Add import** in `model_tools.py` `_discover_tools()` list.","","**3. Add to `toolsets.py`** — either `_GAUSS_CORE_TOOLS` (all platforms) or a new toolset.","","The registry handles schema collection, dispatch, availability checking, and error wrapping. All handlers MUST return a JSON string.","","**Agent-level tools** (todo, memory): intercepted by `run_agent.py` before `handle_function_call()`. See `todo_tool.py` for the pattern.","","---","","## Adding Configuration","","### config.yaml options:","1. Add to `DEFAULT_CONFIG` in `gauss_cli/config.py`","2. Bump `_config_version` (currently 9) to trigger migration for existing users","","### .env variables:","1. Add to `OPTIONAL_ENV_VARS` in `gauss_cli/config.py` with metadata:","```python","\"NEW_API_KEY\": {","    \"description\": \"What it's for\",","    \"prompt\": \"Display name\",","    \"url\": \"https://...\",","    \"password\": True,","    \"category\": \"tool\",  # provider, tool, messaging, setting","},","```","","### Config loaders (two separate systems):","","| Loader | Used by | Location |","|--------|---------|----------|","| `load_cli_config()` | CLI mode | `cli.py` |","| `load_config()` | `gauss tools`, `gauss setup` | `gauss_cli/config.py` |","| Direct YAML load | Gateway | `gateway/run.py` |","","---","","## Skin/Theme System","","The skin engine (`gauss_cli/skin_engine.py`) provides data-driven CLI visual customization. Skins are **pure data** — no code changes needed to add a new skin.","","### Architecture","","```","gauss_cli/skin_engine.py    # SkinConfig dataclass, built-in skins, YAML loader","~/.gauss/skins/*.yaml       # User-installed custom skins (drop-in)","```","","- `init_skin_from_config()` — called at CLI startup, reads `display.skin` from config","- `get_active_skin()` — returns cached `SkinConfig` for the current skin","- `set_active_skin(name)` — switches skin at runtime (used by `/skin` command)","- `load_skin(name)` — loads from user skins first, then built-ins, then falls back to default","- Missing skin values inherit from the `default` skin automatically","","### What skins customize","","| Element | Skin Key | Used By |","|---------|----------|---------|","| Banner panel border | `colors.banner_border` | `banner.py` |","| Banner panel title | `colors.banner_title` | `banner.py` |","| Banner section headers | `colors.banner_accent` | `banner.py` |","| Banner dim text | `colors.banner_dim` | `banner.py` |","| Banner body text | `colors.banner_text` | `banner.py` |","| Response box border | `colors.response_border` | `cli.py` |","| Spinner faces (waiting) | `spinner.waiting_faces` | `display.py` |","| Spinner faces (thinking) | `spinner.thinking_faces` | `display.py` |","| Spinner verbs | `spinner.thinking_verbs` | `display.py` |","| Spinner wings (optional) | `spinner.wings` | `display.py` |","| Tool output prefix | `tool_prefix` | `display.py` |","| Per-tool emojis | `tool_emojis` | `display.py` → `get_tool_emoji()` |","| Agent name | `branding.agent_name` | `banner.py`, `cli.py` |","| Welcome message | `branding.welcome` | `cli.py` |","| Response box label | `branding.response_label` | `cli.py` |","| Prompt symbol | `branding.prompt_symbol` | `cli.py` |","","### Built-in skins","","- `default` — Classic Gauss gold/kawaii (the current look)","- `ares` — Crimson/bronze war-god theme with custom spinner wings","- `mono` — Clean grayscale monochrome","- `slate` — Cool blue developer-focused theme","","### Adding a built-in skin","","Add to `_BUILTIN_SKINS` dict in `gauss_cli/skin_engine.py`:","","```python","\"mytheme\": {","    \"name\": \"mytheme\",","    \"description\": \"Short description\",","    \"colors\": { ... },","    \"spinner\": { ... },","    \"branding\": { ... },","    \"tool_prefix\": \"┊\",","},","```","","### User skins (YAML)","","Users create `~/.gauss/skins/\u003cname\u003e.yaml`:","","```yaml","name: cyberpunk","description: Neon-soaked terminal theme","","colors:","  banner_border: \"#FF00FF\"","  banner_title: \"#00FFFF\"","  banner_accent: \"#FF1493\"","","spinner:","  thinking_verbs: [\"jacking in\", \"decrypting\", \"uploading\"]","  wings:","    - [\"⟨⚡\", \"⚡⟩\"]","","branding:","  agent_name: \"Cyber Agent\"","  response_label: \" ⚡ Cyber \"","","tool_prefix: \"▏\"","```","","Activate with `/skin cyberpunk` or `display.skin: cyberpunk` in config.yaml.","","---","","## Important Policies","### Prompt Caching Must Not Break","","Gauss-Agent ensures caching remains valid throughout a conversation. **Do NOT implement changes that would:**","- Alter past context mid-conversation","- Change toolsets mid-conversation","- Reload memories or rebuild system prompts mid-conversation","","Cache-breaking forces dramatically higher costs. The ONLY time we alter context is during context compression.","","### Working Directory Behavior","- **CLI**: Uses current directory (`.` → `os.getcwd()`)","- **Messaging**: Uses `MESSAGING_CWD` env var (default: home directory)","","### Background Process Notifications (Gateway)","","When `terminal(background=true, check_interval=...)` is used, the gateway runs a watcher that","pushes status updates to the user's chat. Control verbosity with `display.background_process_notifications`","in config.yaml (or `GAUSS_BACKGROUND_NOTIFICATIONS` env var):","","- `all` — running-output updates + final message (default)","- `result` — only the final completion message","- `error` — only the final message when exit code != 0","- `off` — no watcher messages at all","","---","","## Known Pitfalls","","### DO NOT use `simple_term_menu` for interactive menus","Rendering bugs in tmux/iTerm2 — ghosting on scroll. Use `curses` (stdlib) instead. See `gauss_cli/tools_config.py` for the pattern.","","### DO NOT use `\\033[K` (ANSI erase-to-EOL) in spinner/display code","Leaks as literal `?[K` text under `prompt_toolkit`'s `patch_stdout`. Use space-padding: `f\"\\r{line}{' ' * pad}\"`.","","### `_last_resolved_tool_names` is a process-global in `model_tools.py`","When subagents overwrite this global, `execute_code` calls after delegation may fail with missing tool imports. Known bug.","","### Tests must not write to `~/.gauss/`","The `_isolate_gauss_home` autouse fixture in `tests/conftest.py` redirects `GAUSS_HOME` to a temp dir. Never hardcode `~/.gauss/` paths in tests.","","---","","## Testing","","```bash","source .venv/bin/activate","python -m pytest tests/ -q          # Full suite (~3000 tests, ~3 min)","python -m pytest tests/test_model_tools.py -q   # Toolset resolution","python -m pytest tests/test_cli_init.py -q       # CLI config loading","python -m pytest tests/gateway/ -q               # Gateway tests","python -m pytest tests/tools/ -q                 # Tool-level tests","```","","Always run the full suite before pushing changes."],"stylingDirectives":[[[0,33,"pl-mh"],[2,33,"pl-en"]],[],[],[],[[0,26,"pl-mh"],[3,26,"pl-en"]],[],[[0,3,"pl-s"],[3,7,"pl-en"]],[[0,6,"pl-c1"],[27,66,"pl-c"],[27,28,"pl-c"]],[[0,3,"pl-s"]],[],[[0,20,"pl-mh"],[3,20,"pl-en"]],[],[[0,3,"pl-s"],[3,3,"pl-c1"]],[[0,12,"pl-c1"]],[[0,66,"pl-c1"]],[[0,89,"pl-c1"]],[[0,71,"pl-c1"]],[[0,73,"pl-c1"]],[[0,73,"pl-c1"]],[[0,43,"pl-c1"]],[[0,54,"pl-c1"]],[[0,56,"pl-c1"]],[[0,56,"pl-c1"]],[[0,76,"pl-c1"]],[[0,71,"pl-c1"]],[[0,70,"pl-c1"]],[[0,73,"pl-c1"]],[[0,57,"pl-c1"]],[[0,52,"pl-c1"]],[[0,65,"pl-c1"]],[[0,72,"pl-c1"]],[[0,77,"pl-c1"]],[[0,72,"pl-c1"]],[[0,52,"pl-c1"]],[[0,72,"pl-c1"]],[[0,79,"pl-c1"]],[[0,77,"pl-c1"]],[[0,77,"pl-c1"]],[[0,63,"pl-c1"]],[[0,58,"pl-c1"]],[[0,68,"pl-c1"]],[[0,79,"pl-c1"]],[[0,55,"pl-c1"]],[[0,50,"pl-c1"]],[[0,59,"pl-c1"]],[[0,56,"pl-c1"]],[[0,52,"pl-c1"]],[[0,58,"pl-c1"]],[[0,53,"pl-c1"]],[[0,47,"pl-c1"]],[[0,52,"pl-c1"]],[[0,95,"pl-c1"]],[[0,54,"pl-c1"]],[[0,71,"pl-c1"]],[[0,67,"pl-c1"]],[[0,95,"pl-c1"]],[[0,78,"pl-c1"]],[[0,61,"pl-c1"]],[[0,62,"pl-c1"]],[[0,54,"pl-c1"]],[[0,53,"pl-c1"]],[[0,0,"pl-c1"],[0,3,"pl-s"]],[],[[0,2,"pl-s"],[14,16,"pl-s"],[17,18,"pl-s"],[18,38,"pl-c1"],[38,39,"pl-s"],[52,53,"pl-s"],[53,66,"pl-c1"],[66,67,"pl-s"]],[],[[0,24,"pl-mh"],[3,24,"pl-en"]],[],[[0,3,"pl-s"],[3,3,"pl-c1"]],[[0,57,"pl-c1"]],[[0,8,"pl-c1"]],[[0,59,"pl-c1"]],[[0,8,"pl-c1"]],[[0,66,"pl-c1"]],[[0,8,"pl-c1"]],[[0,52,"pl-c1"]],[[0,0,"pl-c1"],[0,3,"pl-s"]],[],[[0,3,"pl-ms"]],[],[[0,31,"pl-mh"],[3,31,"pl-en"]],[],[[0,3,"pl-s"],[3,9,"pl-en"]],[[0,5,"pl-k"],[6,13,"pl-en"]],[[4,7,"pl-k"],[8,16,"pl-c1"],[17,21,"pl-smi"],[17,21,"pl-smi"]],[[8,13,"pl-smi"],[15,18,"pl-c1"],[19,20,"pl-k"],[21,48,"pl-s"],[21,22,"pl-pds"],[47,48,"pl-pds"]],[[8,22,"pl-smi"],[24,27,"pl-c1"],[28,29,"pl-k"],[30,32,"pl-c1"]],[[8,24,"pl-smi"],[26,30,"pl-c1"],[31,32,"pl-k"],[33,37,"pl-c1"]],[[8,25,"pl-smi"],[27,31,"pl-c1"],[32,33,"pl-k"],[34,38,"pl-c1"]],[[8,18,"pl-smi"],[20,24,"pl-c1"],[25,26,"pl-k"],[27,32,"pl-c1"]],[[8,25,"pl-smi" <div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Project Structure</h2><a id="user-content-project-structure" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Project Structure" href="#project-structure"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="gauss-agent/
├── run_agent.py          # AIAgent class — core conversation loop
├── model_tools.py        # Tool orchestration, _discover_tools(), handle_function_call()
├── toolsets.py           # Toolset definitions, _GAUSS_CORE_TOOLS list
├── cli.py                # GaussCLI class — interactive CLI orchestrator
├── gauss_state.py       # SessionDB — SQLite session store (FTS5 search)
├── agent/                # Agent internals
│   ├── prompt_builder.py     # System prompt assembly
│   ├── context_compressor.py # Auto context compression
│   ├── prompt_caching.py     # Anthropic prompt caching
│   ├── auxiliary_client.py   # Auxiliary LLM client (vision, summarization)
│   ├── model_metadata.py     # Model context lengths, token estimation
│   ├── display.py            # KawaiiSpinner, tool preview formatting
│   ├── skill_commands.py     # Skill slash commands (shared CLI/gateway)
│   └── trajectory.py         # Trajectory saving helpers
├── gauss_cli/           # CLI subcommands and setup
│   ├── main.py           # Entry point — all `gauss` subcommands
│   ├── config.py         # DEFAULT_CONFIG, OPTIONAL_ENV_VARS, migration
│   ├── commands.py       # Slash command definitions + SlashCommandCompleter
│   ├── callbacks.py      # Terminal callbacks (clarify, sudo, approval)
│   ├── setup.py          # Interactive setup wizard
│   ├── skin_engine.py    # Skin/theme engine — CLI visual customization
│   ├── skills_config.py  # `gauss skills` — enable/disable skills per platform
│   ├── tools_config.py   # `gauss tools` — enable/disable tools per platform
│   ├── skills_hub.py     # `/skills` slash command (search, browse, install)
│   ├── models.py         # Model catalog, provider model lists
│   └── auth.py           # Provider credential resolution
├── tools/                # Tool implementations (one file per tool)
│   ├── registry.py       # Central tool registry (schemas, handlers, dispatch)
│   ├── approval.py       # Dangerous command detection
│   ├── terminal_tool.py  # Terminal orchestration
│   ├── process_registry.py # Background process management
│   ├── file_tools.py     # File read/write/search/patch
│   ├── web_tools.py      # Firecrawl search/extract
│   ├── browser_tool.py   # Browserbase browser automation
│   ├── code_execution_tool.py # execute_code sandbox
│   ├── delegate_tool.py  # Subagent delegation
│   ├── mcp_tool.py       # MCP client (~1050 lines)
│   └── environments/     # Terminal backends (local, docker, ssh, modal, daytona, singularity)
├── gateway/              # Messaging platform gateway
│   ├── run.py            # Main loop, slash commands, message dispatch
│   ├── session.py        # SessionStore — conversation persistence
│   └── platforms/        # Adapters: telegram, discord, slack, whatsapp, homeassistant, signal
├── acp_adapter/          # ACP server (VS Code / Zed / JetBrains integration)
├── cron/                 # Scheduler (jobs.py, scheduler.py)
├── environments/         # RL training environments (Atropos)
├── tests/                # Pytest suite (~3000 tests)
└── batch_runner.py       # Parallel batch processing"><pre class="notranslate"><code>gauss-agent/

<p dir="auto"><strong>User config:</strong> <code>~/.gauss/config.yaml</code> (settings), <code>~/.gauss/.env</code> (API keys)</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">File Dependency Chain</h2><a id="user-content-file-dependency-chain" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: File Dependency Chain" href="#file-dependency-chain"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="tools/registry.py  (no deps — imported by all tool files)
       ↑
tools/*.py  (each calls registry.register() at import time)
       ↑
model_tools.py  (imports tools/registry + triggers tool discovery)
       ↑
run_agent.py, cli.py, batch_runner.py, environments/"><pre class="notranslate"><code>tools/registry.py  (no deps — imported by all tool files)
       ↑
tools/*.py  (each calls registry.register() at import time)
       ↑
model_tools.py  (imports tools/registry + triggers tool discovery)
       ↑
run_agent.py, cli.py, batch_runner.py, environments/
</code></pre></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">AIAgent Class (run_agent.py)</h2><a id="user-content-aiagent-class-run_agentpy" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: AIAgent Class (run_agent.py)" href="#aiagent-class-run_agentpy"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="class AIAgent:
    def __init__(self,
        model: str = &quot;anthropic/claude-opus-4.6&quot;,

    def chat(self, message: str) -&gt; str:

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Agent Loop</h3><a id="user-content-agent-loop" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Agent Loop" href="#agent-loop"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The core loop is inside <code>run_conversation()</code> — entirely synchronous:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="while api_call_count &lt; self.max_iterations and self.iteration_budget.remaining &gt; 0:
    response = client.chat.completions.create(model=model, messages=messages, tools=tool_schemas)
    if response.tool_calls:
        for tool_call in response.tool_calls:
            result = handle_function_call(tool_call.name, tool_call.args, task_id)
            messages.append(tool_result_message(result))
        api_call_count += 1
    else:
        return response.content"><pre><span class="pl-k">while</span> <span class="pl-s1">api_call_count</span> <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span> <span class="pl-s1">self</span>.<span class="pl-c1">max_iterations</span> <span class="pl-c1">and</span> <span class="pl-s1">self</span>.<span class="pl-c1">iteration_budget</span>.<span class="pl-c1">remaining</span> <span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>:
    <span class="pl-s1">response</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">client</span>.<span class="pl-c1">chat</span>.<span class="pl-c1">completions</span>.<span class="pl-c1">create</span>(<span class="pl-s1">model</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">model</span>, <span class="pl-s1">messages</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">messages</span>, <span class="pl-s1">tools</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">tool_schemas</span>)
    <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-s1">response</span>.<span class="pl-c1">tool_calls</span>:
        <span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s1">tool_call</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-s1">response</span>.<span class="pl-c1">tool_calls</span>:
            <span class="pl-s1">result</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">handle_function_call</span>(<span class="pl-s1">tool_call</span>.<span class="pl-c1">name</span>, <span class="pl-s1">tool_call</span>.<span class="pl-c1">args</span>, <span class="pl-s1">task_id</span>)
            <span class="pl-s1">messages</span>.<span class="pl-c1">append</span>(<span class="pl-en">tool_result_message</span>(<span class="pl-s1">result</span>))
        <span class="pl-s1">api_call_count</span> <span class="pl-c1">+=</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span>
    <span class="pl-k">else</span>:
        <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">response</span>.<span class="pl-c1">content</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Messages follow OpenAI format: <code>{"role": "system/user/assistant/tool", ...}</code>. Reasoning content is stored in <code>assistant_msg["reasoning"]</code>.</p>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">CLI Architecture (cli.py)</h2><a id="user-content-cli-architecture-clipy" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: CLI Architecture (cli.py)" href="#cli-architecture-clipy"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Rich</strong> for banner/panels, <strong>prompt_toolkit</strong> for input with autocomplete</li>
<li><strong>KawaiiSpinner</strong> (<code>agent/display.py</code>) — animated faces during API calls, <code>┊</code> activity feed for tool results</li>
<li><code>load_cli_config()</code> in cli.py merges hardcoded defaults + user config YAML</li>
<li><strong>Skin engine</strong> (<code>gauss_cli/skin_engine.py</code>) — data-driven CLI theming; initialized from <code>display.skin</code> config key at startup; skins customize banner colors, spinner faces/verbs/wings, tool prefix, response box, branding text</li>
<li><code>process_command()</code> is a method on <code>GaussCLI</code> (not in commands.py)</li>
<li>Skill slash commands: <code>agent/skill_commands.py</code> scans <code>~/.gauss/skills/</code>, injects as <strong>user message</strong> (not system prompt) to preserve prompt caching</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Adding CLI Commands</h3><a id="user-content-adding-cli-commands" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Adding CLI Commands" href="#adding-cli-commands"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Add to <code>COMMANDS</code> dict in <code>gauss_cli/commands.py</code></li>
<li>Add handler in <code>GaussCLI.process_command()</code> in <code>cli.py</code></li>
<li>For persistent settings, use <code>save_config_value()</code> in <code>cli.py</code></li>
</ol>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Adding New Tools</h2><a id="user-content-adding-new-tools" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Adding New Tools" href="#adding-new-tools"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Requires changes in <strong>3 files</strong>:</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>1. Create <code>tools/your_tool.py</code>:</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="import json, os
from tools.registry import registry

def check_requirements() -&gt; bool:
    return bool(os.getenv(&quot;EXAMPLE_API_KEY&quot;))

def example_tool(param: str, task_id: str = None) -&gt; str:
    return json.dumps({&quot;success&quot;: True, &quot;data&quot;: &quot;...&quot;})

registry.register(
    name=&quot;example_tool&quot;,
    toolset=&quot;example&quot;,
    schema={&quot;name&quot;: &quot;example_tool&quot;, &quot;description&quot;: &quot;...&quot;, &quot;parameters&quot;: {...}},
    handler=lambda args, **kw: example_tool(param=args.get(&quot;param&quot;, &quot;&quot;), task_id=kw.get(&quot;task_id&quot;)),
    check_fn=check_requirements,
    requires_env=[&quot;EXAMPLE_API_KEY&quot;],
)"><pre><span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">json</span>, <span class="pl-s1">os</span>
<span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">tools</span>.<span class="pl-s1">registry</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">registry</span>

<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">check_requirements</span>() <span class="pl-c1">-&gt;</span> <span class="pl-smi">bool</span>:
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-en">bool</span>(<span class="pl-s1">os</span>.<span class="pl-c1">getenv</span>(<span class="pl-s">"EXAMPLE_API_KEY"</span>))

<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">example_tool</span>(<span class="pl-s1">param</span>: <span class="pl-smi">str</span>, <span class="pl-s1">task_id</span>: <span class="pl-smi">str</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">None</span>) <span class="pl-c1">-&gt;</span> <span class="pl-smi">str</span>:
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">json</span>.<span class="pl-c1">dumps</span>({<span class="pl-s">"success"</span>: <span class="pl-c1">True</span>, <span class="pl-s">"data"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"..."</span>})

<span class="pl-s1">registry</span>.<span class="pl-c1">register</span>(
    <span class="pl-s1">name</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"example_tool"</span>,
    <span class="pl-s1">toolset</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"example"</span>,
    <span class="pl-s1">schema</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span>{<span class="pl-s">"name"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"example_tool"</span>, <span class="pl-s">"description"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"..."</span>, <span class="pl-s">"parameters"</span>: {...}},
    <span class="pl-s1">handler</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-k">lambda</span> <span class="pl-s1">args</span>, <span class="pl-c1">**</span><span class="pl-s1">kw</span>: <span class="pl-en">example_tool</span>(<span class="pl-s1">param</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">args</span>.<span class="pl-c1">get</span>(<span class="pl-s">"param"</span>, <span class="pl-s">""</span>), <span class="pl-s1">task_id</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">kw</span>.<span class="pl-c1">get</span>(<span class="pl-s">"task_id"</span>)),
    <span class="pl-s1">check_fn</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">check_requirements</span>,
    <span class="pl-s1">requires_env</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span>[<span class="pl-s">"EXAMPLE_API_KEY"</span>],
)</pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>2. Add import</strong> in <code>model_tools.py</code> <code>_discover_tools()</code> list.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>3. Add to <code>toolsets.py</code></strong> — either <code>_GAUSS_CORE_TOOLS</code> (all platforms) or a new toolset.</p>
<p dir="auto">The registry handles schema collection, dispatch, availability checking, and error wrapping. All handlers MUST return a JSON string.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Agent-level tools</strong> (todo, memory): intercepted by <code>run_agent.py</code> before <code>handle_function_call()</code>. See <code>todo_tool.py</code> for the pattern.</p>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Adding Configuration</h2><a id="user-content-adding-configuration" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Adding Configuration" href="#adding-configuration"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">config.yaml options:</h3><a id="user-content-configyaml-options" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: config.yaml options:" href="#configyaml-options"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Add to <code>DEFAULT_CONFIG</code> in <code>gauss_cli/config.py</code></li>
<li>Bump <code>_config_version</code> (currently 9) to trigger migration for existing users</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">.env variables:</h3><a id="user-content-env-variables" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: .env variables:" href="#env-variables"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Add to <code>OPTIONAL_ENV_VARS</code> in <code>gauss_cli/config.py</code> with metadata:</li>
</ol>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="&quot;NEW_API_KEY&quot;: {
    &quot;description&quot;: &quot;What it's for&quot;,
    &quot;prompt&quot;: &quot;Display name&quot;,
    &quot;url&quot;: &quot;https://...&quot;,
    &quot;password&quot;: True,
    &quot;category&quot;: &quot;tool&quot;,  # provider, tool, messaging, setting
},"><pre><span class="pl-s">"NEW_API_KEY"</span>: {
    <span class="pl-s">"description"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"What it's for"</span>,
    <span class="pl-s">"prompt"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Display name"</span>,
    <span class="pl-s">"url"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"https://..."</span>,
    <span class="pl-s">"password"</span>: <span class="pl-c1">True</span>,
    <span class="pl-s">"category"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"tool"</span>,  <span class="pl-c"># provider, tool, messaging, setting</span>
},</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Config loaders (two separate systems):</h3><a id="user-content-config-loaders-two-separate-systems" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Config loaders (two separate systems):" href="#config-loaders-two-separate-systems"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Skin/Theme System</h2><a id="user-content-skintheme-system" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Skin/Theme System" href="#skintheme-system"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The skin engine (<code>gauss_cli/skin_engine.py</code>) provides data-driven CLI visual customization. Skins are <strong>pure data</strong> — no code changes needed to add a new skin.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Architecture</h3><a id="user-content-architecture" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Architecture" href="#architecture"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="gauss_cli/skin_engine.py    # SkinConfig dataclass, built-in skins, YAML loader
~/.gauss/skins/*.yaml       # User-installed custom skins (drop-in)"><pre class="notranslate"><code>gauss_cli/skin_engine.py    # SkinConfig dataclass, built-in skins, YAML loader
~/.gauss/skins/*.yaml       # User-installed custom skins (drop-in)
</code></pre></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>init_skin_from_config()</code> — called at CLI startup, reads <code>display.skin</code> from config</li>
<li><code>get_active_skin()</code> — returns cached <code>SkinConfig</code> for the current skin</li>
<li><code>set_active_skin(name)</code> — switches skin at runtime (used by <code>/skin</code> command)</li>
<li><code>load_skin(name)</code> — loads from user skins first, then built-ins, then falls back to default</li>
<li>Missing skin values inherit from the <code>default</code> skin automatically</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">What skins customize</h3><a id="user-content-what-skins-customize" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: What skins customize" href="#what-skins-customize"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Built-in skins</h3><a id="user-content-built-in-skins" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Built-in skins" href="#built-in-skins"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>default</code> — Classic Gauss gold/kawaii (the current look)</li>
<li><code>ares</code> — Crimson/bronze war-god theme with custom spinner wings</li>
<li><code>mono</code> — Clean grayscale monochrome</li>
<li><code>slate</code> — Cool blue developer-focused theme</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Adding a built-in skin</h3><a id="user-content-adding-a-built-in-skin" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Adding a built-in skin" href="#adding-a-built-in-skin"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Add to <code>_BUILTIN_SKINS</code> dict in <code>gauss_cli/skin_engine.py</code>:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="&quot;mytheme&quot;: {
    &quot;name&quot;: &quot;mytheme&quot;,
    &quot;description&quot;: &quot;Short description&quot;,
    &quot;colors&quot;: { ... },
    &quot;spinner&quot;: { ... },
    &quot;branding&quot;: { ... },
    &quot;tool_prefix&quot;: &quot;┊&quot;,
},"><pre><span class="pl-s">"mytheme"</span>: {
    <span class="pl-s">"name"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"mytheme"</span>,
    <span class="pl-s">"description"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Short description"</span>,
    <span class="pl-s">"colors"</span>: { ... },
    <span class="pl-s">"spinner"</span>: { ... },
    <span class="pl-s">"branding"</span>: { ... },
    <span class="pl-s">"tool_prefix"</span>: <span class="pl-s">"┊"</span>,
},</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">User skins (YAML)</h3><a id="user-content-user-skins-yaml" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: User skins (YAML)" href="#user-skins-yaml"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Users create <code>~/.gauss/skins/&lt;name&gt;.yaml</code>:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-yaml notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="name: cyberpunk
description: Neon-soaked terminal theme

colors:
  banner_border: &quot;#FF00FF&quot;
  banner_title: &quot;#00FFFF&quot;
  banner_accent: &quot;#FF1493&quot;

  thinking_verbs: [&quot;jacking in&quot;, &quot;decrypting&quot;, &quot;uploading&quot;]

    - [&quot;⟨⚡&quot;, &quot;⚡⟩&quot;]

branding:
  agent_name: &quot;Cyber Agent&quot;
  response_label: &quot; ⚡ Cyber &quot;

tool_prefix: &quot;▏&quot;"><pre><span class="pl-ent">name</span>: <span class="pl-s">cyberpunk</span>
<span class="pl-ent">description</span>: <span class="pl-s">Neon-soaked terminal theme</span>

<span class="pl-ent">colors</span>:
  <span class="pl-ent">banner_border</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>#FF00FF<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
  <span class="pl-ent">banner_title</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>#00FFFF<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
  <span class="pl-ent">banner_accent</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>#FF1493<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>

<span class="pl-ent">spinner</span>:
  <span class="pl-ent">thinking_verbs</span>: <span class="pl-s">["jacking in", "decrypting", "uploading"]</span>
  <span class="pl-ent">wings</span>:
    - <span class="pl-s">["⟨⚡", "⚡⟩"]</span>

<span class="pl-ent">branding</span>:
  <span class="pl-ent">agent_name</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Cyber Agent<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
  <span class="pl-ent">response_label</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> ⚡ Cyber <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>

<span class="pl-ent">tool_prefix</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>▏<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Activate with <code>/skin cyberpunk</code> or <code>display.skin: cyberpunk</code> in config.yaml.</p>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Important Policies</h2><a id="user-content-important-policies" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Important Policies" href="#important-policies"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Prompt Caching Must Not Break</h3><a id="user-content-prompt-caching-must-not-break" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Prompt Caching Must Not Break" href="#prompt-caching-must-not-break"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Gauss-Agent ensures caching remains valid throughout a conversation. <strong>Do NOT implement changes that would:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Alter past context mid-conversation</li>
<li>Change toolsets mid-conversation</li>
<li>Reload memories or rebuild system prompts mid-conversation</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">Cache-breaking forces dramatically higher costs. The ONLY time we alter context is during context compression.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Working Directory Behavior</h3><a id="user-content-working-directory-behavior" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Working Directory Behavior" href="#working-directory-behavior"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>CLI</strong>: Uses current directory (<code>.</code> → <code>os.getcwd()</code>)</li>
<li><strong>Messaging</strong>: Uses <code>MESSAGING_CWD</code> env var (default: home directory)</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Background Process Notifications (Gateway)</h3><a id="user-content-background-process-notifications-gateway" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Background Process Notifications (Gateway)" href="#background-process-notifications-gateway"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">When <code>terminal(background=true, check_interval=...)</code> is used, the gateway runs a watcher that
pushes status updates to the user's chat. Control verbosity with <code>display.background_process_notifications</code>
in config.yaml (or <code>GAUSS_BACKGROUND_NOTIFICATIONS</code> env var):</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>all</code> — running-output updates + final message (default)</li>
<li><code>result</code> — only the final completion message</li>
<li><code>error</code> — only the final message when exit code != 0</li>
<li><code>off</code> — no watcher messages at all</li>
</ul>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Known Pitfalls</h2><a id="user-content-known-pitfalls" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Known Pitfalls" href="#known-pitfalls"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">DO NOT use <code>simple_term_menu</code> for interactive menus</h3><a id="user-content-do-not-use-simple_term_menu-for-interactive-menus" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: DO NOT use simple_term_menu for interactive menus" href="#do-not-use-simple_term_menu-for-interactive-menus"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Rendering bugs in tmux/iTerm2 — ghosting on scroll. Use <code>curses</code> (stdlib) instead. See <code>gauss_cli/tools_config.py</code> for the pattern.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">DO NOT use <code>\033[K</code> (ANSI erase-to-EOL) in spinner/display code</h3><a id="user-content-do-not-use-033k-ansi-erase-to-eol-in-spinnerdisplay-code" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: DO NOT use \033[K (ANSI erase-to-EOL) in spinner/display code" href="#do-not-use-033k-ansi-erase-to-eol-in-spinnerdisplay-code"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Leaks as literal <code>?[K</code> text under <code>prompt_toolkit</code>'s <code>patch_stdout</code>. Use space-padding: <code>f"\r{line}{' ' * pad}"</code>.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><code>_last_resolved_tool_names</code> is a process-global in <code>model_tools.py</code></h3><a id="user-content-_last_resolved_tool_names-is-a-process-global-in-model_toolspy" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: _last_resolved_tool_names is a process-global in model_tools.py" href="#_last_resolved_tool_names-is-a-process-global-in-model_toolspy"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">When subagents overwrite this global, <code>execute_code</code> calls after delegation may fail with missing tool imports. Known bug.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Tests must not write to <code>~/.gauss/</code></h3><a id="user-content-tests-must-not-write-to-gauss" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Tests must not write to ~/.gauss/" href="#tests-must-not-write-to-gauss"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The <code>_isolate_gauss_home</code> autouse fixture in <code>tests/conftest.py</code> redirects <code>GAUSS_HOME</code> to a temp dir. Never hardcode <code>~/.gauss/</code> paths in tests.</p>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Testing</h2><a id="user-content-testing" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Testing" href="#testing"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
